The way we work now – giving our administration a call from the car with questions like these – is not a viable way of working and should be a thing of the past. This way of doing business was okay 5 years ago, we had fewer external service employees then.”\r\nFor service mechanics:\r\n“Sometimes it takes several weeks before all service receipts are turned in and we can start the billing process.
